[ACTION] east [STATE] Nave You enter the Abbey and pause in the Nave, struck by the sheer magnificence of the building. Massive Purbeck columns march the length of the Nave, and they rise in perfect proportion to meet each other in a series of pointed arches that are the hallmark of the Gothic style.
